\"miroir:leader_lease\";\n421\t\n422\t        // Use SET with NX (only set if not exists) and EX (expiration)\n423\t        let ttl = (lease.expires_at - lease.acquired_at) / 1000;\n424\t job = self\n                .job_get(&job_id)\n                .await?\n                .ok_or_else(|| TaskStoreError::NotFound(job_id.clone()))?;\n\n            // Update status\n }\n489\t\n490\t    async fn job_dequeue(&self, worker_id: &str) -> Result<Option<Job>> {\n491\t        // Start a transaction\n492\t        let conn = self\n493\t            .conn\n494\t            .lock()\n495\t            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n496\t        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n497\t\n498\t        let now = chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64;\n499\t\n500\t        // Find and claim a job\n501\t        let job_id: Option<String> = tx\n502\t            .query_row(\n503\t                \"SELECT job_id FROM jobs WHERE status = 'Enqueued' ORDER BY created_at ASC LIMIT 1\",\n504\t                [],\n505\t                |row| row.get(0),\n506\t            )\n507\t            .ok();\n508\t\n509\t        if let Some(ref job_id) = job_id {\n510\t            tx.execute(\n511\t                \"UPDATE jobs SET status = 'Processing', worker_id = ?1, started_at = ?2 WHERE job_id = ?3\",\n512\t                [\n513\t                    &worker_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n514\t                    &now as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n515\t                    job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n516\t                ],\n517\t            )?;\n518\t\n519\t            // Fetch the updated job\n520\t            let job: Job = tx.query_row(\n521\t                \"SELECT job_id, job_type, parameters, status, worker_id, result, error, created_at, started_at, completed_at\n522\t                 FROM jobs WHERE job_id = ?1\",\n523\t                [job_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n524\t                |row| {\n525\t                    Ok(Job {\n526\t                        job_id: row.get(0)?,\n527\t                        job_type: row.get(1)?,\n528\t                        parameters: row.get(2)?,\n529\t                        status: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n530\t                        worker_id: {\n531\t                            let worker: String = row.get(4)?;\n532\t                            if worker.is_empty() { None } else { Some(worker) }\n533\t                        },\n534\t                        result: {\n535\t                            let result: String = row.get(5)?;\n536\t                            if result.is_empty() { None } else { Some(result) }\n537\t                        },\n538\t                        error: {\n539\t                            let error: String = row.get(6)?;\n540\t                            if error.is_empty() { None } else { Some(error) }\n541\t                        },\n542\t                        created_at: row.get(7)?,\n543\t                        started_at: {\n544\t                            let started: i64 = row.get(8)?;\n545\t                            if started == 0 { None } else { Some(started as u64) }\n546\t                        },\n547\t                        completed_at: {\n548\t                            let completed: i64 = row.get(9)?;\n549\t                            if completed == 0 { None } else { Some(completed as u64) }\n550\t                        },\n551\t                    })\n552\t                },\n553\t            )?;\n554\t\n555\t            tx.commit()?;\n556\t            Ok(Some(job))\n557\t        } else {\n558\t            tx.commit()?;\n559\t            Ok(None)\n560\t        }\n561\t    }\n562\t\n563\t    async fn job_update_status(\n564\t        &self,\n565\t        job_id: &str,\n566\t        status: JobStatus,\n567\t        result: Option<&str>,\n568\t    ) ->  self.query_map(&sql, &params, |row| {\n            Ok(Job {\n                job_id: row.get(0)?,\n                job_type: row.get(1)?,\n                parameters: row.get(2)?,\n                status: row.get::<_, String>(3)?.parse().map_err(parse_error)?,\n                worker_id: {\n                    let worker: String = row.get(4)?;\n                    if worker.is_empty() {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(worker)\n                    }\n                },\n                result: {\n                    let result: String = row.get(5)?;\n                    if result.is_empty() {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(result)\n                    }\n                },\n                error: {\n                    let error: String = row.get(6)?;\n                    if error.is_empty() {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(error)\n                    }\n                },\n                created_at: row.get(7)?,\n                started_at: {\n                    let started: i64 = row.get(8)?;\n                    if started == 0 {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(started as u64)\n                    }\n                },\n                completed_at: {\n                    let completed: i64 = row.get(9)?;\n                    if completed == 0 {\n                        None\n                    } else {\n                        Some(completed as u64)\n                    }\n                },\n            })\n        })\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_acquire(&self, lease: &LeaderLease) -> Result<bool> {\n        let conn = self\n            .conn\n            .lock()\n            .map_err(|e| TaskStoreError::Internal(e.to_string()))?;\n        let tx = conn.unchecked_transaction()?;\n\n        // Check if there's an existing valid lease\n        let existing: Option<(String, u64)> = tx\n            .query_row(\n                \"SELECT lease_id, expires_at FROM leader_lease WHERE expires_at > ?1\",\n                [&(chrono::Utc::now().timestamp_millis() as u64) as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n                |row| Ok((row.get(0)?, row.get(1)?)),\n            )\n            .ok();\n\n        let acquired = if existing.is_some() {\n            false\n        } else {\n            tx.execute(\n                \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO leader_lease (lease_id, holder, acquired_at, expires_at)\n                 VALUES (?1, ?2, ?3, ?4)\",\n                [\n                    &lease.lease_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql,\n                    &lease.holder,\n                    &lease.acquired_at,\n                    &lease.expires_at,\n                ],\n            )?;\n            true\n        };\n\n        tx.commit()?;\n        Ok(acquired)\n    }\n\n    async fn leader_lease_release(&self, lease_id: &str) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"DELETE FROM leader_lease WHERE lease_id = ?1\",\n            &[&lease_id as &dyn rusqlite::ToSql],\n        )?;\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n },\n            )\n            .ok();\n        Ok(result)\n    }\n\n    async fn canary_upsert(&self, canary: &Canary) -> Result<()> {\n        self.execute(\n            \"INSERT OR REPLACE INTO    conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tasks (\n                miroir_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                status TEXT NOT NULL,\n                node_tasks TEXT NOT NULL,\n                error TEXT\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 2: Node settings version\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS node_settings_version (\n                [index] TEXT NOT NULL,\n                node_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n                version INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                PRIMARY KEY ([index], node_id)\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 3: Aliases\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS aliases (\n                name TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                kind TEXT NOT NULL,\n                current_uid TEXT,\n                target_uids TEXT NOT NULL,\n                version INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 4: Sessions\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sessions (\n                session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                [index] TEXT NOT NULL,\n                settings_version INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                expires_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 5: Idempotency cache\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS idempotency_cache (\n                key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                response TEXT NOT NULL,\n                status_code INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 6: Jobs\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS jobs (\n                job_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                job_type TEXT NOT NULL,\n                parameters TEXT NOT NULL,\n                status TEXT NOT NULL,\n                worker_id TEXT,\n                result TEXT,\n                error TEXT,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                started_at INTEGER,\n                completed_at INTEGER\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 7: Leader lease\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS leader_lease (\n                lease_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                holder TEXT NOT NULL,\n                acquired_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                expires_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 8: Canaries\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS canaries (\n                name TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                [index] TEXT NOT NULL,\n                query TEXT NOT NULL,\n                min_results INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                max_results INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                interval_s INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                enabled INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 9: Canary runs\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS canary_runs (\n                run_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                canary_name TEXT NOT NULL,\n                ran_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                passed INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                result_count INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                error TEXT,\n                latency_ms INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 10: CDC cursors\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS cdc_cursors (\n                sink TEXT NOT NULL,\n                [index] TEXT NOT NULL,\n                cursor TEXT NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                PRIMARY KEY (sink, [index])\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 11: Tenant map\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS tenant_map (\n                api_key TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                tenant_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n                name TEXT NOT NULL,\n                capabilities TEXT NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 12: Rollover policies\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS rollover_policies (\n                name TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                index_pattern TEXT NOT NULL,\n                max_age_days INTEGER,\n                max_size_bytes INTEGER,\n                max_docs INTEGER,\n                enabled INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 13: Search UI config\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS search_ui_config (\n                [index] TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                config TEXT NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                updated_at INTEGER NOT NULL\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        // Table 14: Admin sessions\n        conn.execute(\n            \"CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS admin_sessions (\n                session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,\n                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,\n                created_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                expires_at INTEGER NOT NULL,\n                revoked INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0\n            )\",\n            [],\n        )?;\n\n        Ok(())\n    }\n}\n\n// String conversions for enums\nimpl std::fmt::Display for TaskStatus {\n    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) ->
